  %93 = add i64 %.1245.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.3, %lsr.iv23

  %.1292.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.3 = fadd double %.1292.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.2, %.1291.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.3

  br i1 %.929.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us, label %B373.endif.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us, label %B321.B255.loopexit_crit_edge.split.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.us.split

  store ptr null, ptr %retptr, align 8
  ret i32 0
}

declare i64 @llvm.smin.i64(i64, i64) #3

; Function Attrs: mustprogress nocallback nofree nosync nounwind speculatable willreturn memory(none)
declare i64 @llvm.smax.i64(i64, i64) #3

; Function Attrs: noinline
define linkonce_odr void @NRT_decref(ptr %.1) local_unnamed_addr #4 {
.3:
  %.4 = icmp eq ptr %.1, null
  br i1 %.4, label %common.ret, label %.3.endif, !prof !0

common.ret:                                       ; preds = %.3, %.3.endif
  ret void

.3.endif:                                         ; preds = %.3
  fence release
  %0 = tail call i8 @llvm.x86.atomic.sub.cc.i64(ptr nonnull %.1, i64 1, i32 4)
  %1 = trunc i8 %0 to i1
  br i1 %1, label %.3.endif.if, label %common.ret, !prof !0

.3.endif.if:                                      ; preds = %.3.endif
  fence acquire
  tail call void @NRT_MemInfo_call_dtor(ptr nonnull %.1)
  ret void
}

; Function Attrs: nounwind
declare i8 @llvm.x86.atomic.sub.cc.i64(ptr, i64, i32 immarg) #5

declare void @NRT_MemInfo_call_dtor(ptr) local_unnamed_addr

; Function Attrs: mustprogress nofree noinline norecurse nounwind willreturn memory(argmem: readwrite)
define linkonce_odr void @NRT_incref(ptr %.1) local_unnamed_addr #6 {
.3:
  %.4 = icmp eq ptr %.1, null
  br i1 %.4, label %common.ret, label %.3.endif, !prof !0

common.ret:                                       ; preds = %.3.endif, %.3
  ret void

.3.endif:                                         ; preds = %.3
  %.4.i = atomicrmw add ptr %.1, i64 1 monotonic, align 8
  br label %common.ret
}

; Function Attrs: nocallback nofree nosync nounwind willreturn memory(argmem: readwrite)

; Function Attrs: nocallback nofree nosync nounwind willreturn memory(argmem: readwrite)
